</span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Location\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Cargo\n        </th>\n        <th>\n </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       STS-130 carried\n       <a href="/wiki/Tranquility_(ISS_module)" title="Tranquility (ISS module)">\n        Tranquility\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cupola_(ISS_module)" title="Cupola (ISS module)">\n        Cupola\n       </a>\n       to the International Space Station.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Tranquility was shipped from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Thales_Alenia_Space" title="Thales Alenia Space">\n        Thales Alenia Space\n       </a>\n       facility in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turin,_Italy" title="Turin, Italy">\n        Turin\n       </a>\n       , Italy. It arrived at\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       on 21 May 2009. It was formerly known as Node 3, and was named by a NASA poll.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n id="Shuttle_processing">\n        Shuttle processing\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Shuttle processing">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="2066" height="319" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg/220px-STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg/330px-STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg/440px-STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_Endeavour_Rollout_6.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <i>\n          Endeavour\n         </i>\n         arrives at Pad 39A on 6 January 2010 for the STS 130 mission.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <span class="nowrap">\n        <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n         Space Shuttle\n        </a>\n       </span>\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       was moved from her hangar in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Processing_Facility" title="Orbiter Processing Facility">\n        Orbiter Processing Facility 2\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Vehicle_Assembly_Building" title="Vehicle Assembly Building">\n        Vehicle Assembly Building\n       </a>\n       High bay 1 on 11 December 2009.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-roll-over_13-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-roll-over-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Roll over began at 13:00\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone" title="Eastern Time Zone">\n        EST\n       </a>\n       and was completed 1 hour and 5 minutes later at 14:05 EST.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       moved from the Vehicle Assembly Building to\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center_Launch_Complex_39" title="Kennedy Space Center Launch Complex 39">\n        launch pad 39A\n       </a>\n       . The process started at 04:13 EST on 6 January 2010. Before rolling out to the launch pad, engineers at\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       had an extended preparation time to get\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       ready to move to the launch pad due to the unusually cold weather. The 3.4 miles (5.5\xc2\xa0km) was completed at 10:37 EST. The trip took 6hrs 24min.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Launch_attempts">\n        Launch attempts\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Launch attempts">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The first launch attempt was scheduled for 04:39:00 EST 7 February 2010, but was scrubbed due to clouds over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       . The second launch attempt was successful at 04:14:08 EST (9:14:08 UTC) 8 February 2010. Forecasters originally predicted a 70% chance of favorable launch weather conditions,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but that degraded to 30% hours before the planned launch due to low clouds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-weather30_15-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-weather30-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Attempt\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Planned\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Result\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Turnaround\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Reason\n        </th>\n        <th>\n   Successful\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         0 days, 23 hours, 34 minutes\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         60%\n         <sup    <a href="#cite_note-17">\n           [17]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Mission milestones">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sts130_mission_poster.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="5440" data-file-width="7275" height="172" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Sts130_mission_poster.jpg/230px-Sts130_mission_poster.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Sts130_mission_poster.jpg/345px-Sts130_mission_poster.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ee/Sts130_mission_poster.jpg/460px-Sts130_mission_poster.jpg 2x" width="230"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sts130_mission_poster.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Mission poster\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The mission marked:\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ql_18-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ql-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        161st NASA manned space flight\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        130th shuttle mission since\n        <a href="/wiki/STS-1" title="STS-1">\n         STS-1\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        24th flight of\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        32nd shuttle mission to the ISS\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        10th flight of\n        <i>\n         Endeavour\n        </i>\n        to the ISS\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        1st shuttle flight in 2010\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        105th post-\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Challenger_disaster" title="Space Shuttle Challenger disaster">\n          Challenger\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        mission\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        17th post-\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Columbia_disaster" title="Space Shuttle Columbia disaster">\n          Columbia\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        mission\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        34th night launch of a shuttle, 21st night launch from launch pad 39A\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_timeline">\n        Mission timeline\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Mission timeline">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="8_February_(Flight_Day_1:_Launch)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="8_February_.28Flight_Day_1:_Launch.29">\n        8 February (Flight Day 1: Launch)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 8 February (Flight Day 1: Launch)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_0" style="width:220px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:480px"&gt;&lt;video id="mwe_player_1"     </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">\n         Endeavour\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       launched successfully at 4:14:08 EST (9:14:08 UTC). When\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       lifted off, the space station was traveling about 212 miles over western Romania.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">\n        <a href="#cite_note-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Once in orbit the crew opened the payload bay doors, activated the radiators and deployed the\n       <a href="/wiki/Ku_band" title="Ku band">\n        K\n        <sub>\n         u\n        </sub>\n        band\n       </a>\n       antenna.\n       <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_Patrick" title="Nicholas Patrick">\n        Nick Patrick\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kay_Hire" title="Kay Hire">\n        Kay Hire\n       </a>\n       then proceeded to activate, did a check out of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shuttle_Remote_Manipulator_System" title="Shuttle Remote Manipulator System">\n        Shuttle Robotic Arm\n       </a>\n       (SRMS) and then conducted a survey of the payload bay. The crew was also successful in down-linking imagery and video of the external tank to the ground.\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center" style="max-width: 652px;_width: 652px;">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:15px auto;">\n class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Space Shuttle\n           <i>\n            Endeavour\n           </i>\n           launches from Kennedy Space Center, 8 February 2010.\n          </p>\n  </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           An exhaust cloud engulfs Launch Pad 39A during the launch.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:33.5px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Firing_Room_Four_Launch_Control_Center_STS-130_Launch.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2790" data-file-width="4036" height="83" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Firing_Room_Four_Launch_Control_Center_STS-130_Launch.jpg/120px-Firing_Room_Four_Launch_Control_Center_STS-130_Launch.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Firing_Room_Four_Launch_Control_Center_STS-130_Launch.jpg/180px-Firing_Room_Four_Launch_Control_Center_STS-130_Launch.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/76/Firing_Room_Four_Launch_Control_Center_STS-130_Launch.jpg/240px-Firing_Room_Four_Launch_Control_Center_STS-130_Launch.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charles_F._Bolden,_Jr." title="Charles F. Bolden, Jr.">\n            Bolden\n           </a>\n           , left, congratulates\n           <a href="/wiki/Michael_D._Leinbach" title="Michael D. Leinbach">\n            Leinbach\n           </a>\n           and the launch team in Firing Room Four of the Launch Control Center for a successful launch.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="9_February_(Flight_Day_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="9_February_.28Flight_Day_2.29">\n        9 February (Flight Day 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 9 February (Flight Day 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Most of the crew day was spent on conducting the standard inspection of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_thermal_protection_system" title="Space Shuttle thermal protection system">\n        thermal protection system\n       </a>\n       (TPS).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All six of the crew members participated at one point during this task. Once the inspection process had moved to the port wing, astronauts\n       <a href="/wiki/Robert_L._Behnken" title="Robert L. Behnken">\n        Bob Behnken\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_Patrick" title="Nicholas Patrick">\n        Nick Patrick\n       </a>\n       began working on checking out and preparing the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_mobility_unit" title="Extra-vehicular mobility unit">\n        spacesuits\n       </a>\n       that will be used during the mission\'s three spacewalks. Once the survey of the TPS was complete,\n       <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Robinson" title="Stephen Robinson">\n        Stephen Robinson\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kathryn_Hire" title="Kathryn Hire">\n        Kay Hire\n       </a>\n       , with Bob Behnken joining once his spacesuit tasks were complete, began checking out and preparing the tools that will be used during the rendezvous with the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       (ISS). These tools include a hand-held\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LIDAR" title="LIDAR">\n        LIDAR\n       </a>\n       gun used for finding out the closing rate of the shuttle and distance from the ISS, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orbiter_Docking_System" title="Orbiter Docking System">\n        Orbiter Docking System\n       </a>\n       (ODS) which is the part of the shuttle that connects to the space station and a centerline camera in the ODS to assist the commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/George_Zamka" title="George Zamka">\n        George Zamka\n       </a>\n       during docking.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="10_February_(Flight_Day_3:_Rendezvous_with_ISS)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="10_February_.28Flight_Day_3:_Rendezvous_with_ISS.29">\n        10 February (Flight Day 3: Rendezvous with ISS)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 10 February (Flight Day 3: Rendezvous with ISS)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       During the first part of the crew\'s workday, they performed a series of burns to catch up and dock with the International Space Station (ISS). Once the shuttle was 600 feet (180\xc2\xa0m) below the ISS, commander George Zamka began what is known as the Rendezvous Pitch Maneuver (RPM). During the maneuver, ISS commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jeff_Williams_(astronaut)" title="Jeff Williams (astronaut)">\n        Jeff Williams\n       </a>\n       and flight engineer\n       <a href="/wiki/Oleg_Kotov" title="Oleg Kotov">\n        Oleg Kotov\n       </a>\n       took photos of the shuttle\'s thermal protection system (TPS). Space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       docked with the ISS at 5:26\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       (00:06\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone" title="Eastern Time Zone">\n        EST\n       </a>\n       ). After completing leak checks the hatches between both vehicles were opened at 6:26 UTC (1:26 EST). The joint\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_22" title="Expedition 22">\n        Expedition 22\n       </a>\n       /STS-130 crew conducted the standard welcome ceremony and then conducted their safety brief. Once that was complete commander George Zamka, Bob Behnken and Steve Robinson began transferring the spacesuits Behnken and Nick Patrick will use for the three spacewalks. Also during this time Nick Patrick and ISS flight engineer\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/T.J._Creamer" title="T.J. Creamer">\n        T.J. Creamer\n       </a>\n       picked up the OBSS boom and handed it off to the space shuttle robot arm using the station\'s SSRMS or\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       . The shuttle arm was operated by Kay Hire and pilot\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Terry_Virts" title="Terry Virts">\n        Terry Virts\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center" style="max-width: 652px;_width: 652px;">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_Endeavour_Rendezvous_Pitch_Maneuver_aft_portion.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2040" data-file-width="3072" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/STS-130_Endeavour_Rendezvous_Pitch_Maneuver_aft_portion.jpg/120px-STS-130_Endeavour_Rendezvous_Pitch_Maneuver_aft_portion.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/STS-130_Endeavour_Rendezvous_Pitch_Maneuver_aft_portion.jpg/180px-STS-130_Endeavour_Rendezvous_Pitch_Maneuver_aft_portion.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/13/STS-130_Endeavour_Rendezvous_Pitch_Maneuver_aft_portion.jpg/240px-STS-130_Endeavour_Rendezvous_Pitch_Maneuver_aft_portion.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Image of Endeavour\'s aft section taken during the shuttle\'s approach prior to docking.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_ISS_Approach.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/STS-130_ISS_Approach.jpg/120px-STS-130_ISS_Approach.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/STS-130_ISS_Approach.jpg/180px-STS-130_ISS_Approach.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/STS-130_ISS_Approach.jpg/240px-STS-130_ISS_Approach.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Space Station as photographed by a shuttle crew member.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image"    <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Endeavour\n           </i>\n           approaches the ISS, silhouetted by the Earth\'s horizon.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="11_February_(Flight_Day_4:_Spacewalk_1_preparation)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="11_February_.28Flight_Day_4:_Spacewalk_1_preparation.29">\n        11 February (Flight Day 4: Spacewalk 1 preparation)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 11 February (Flight Day 4: Spacewalk 1 preparation)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 4 saw\n       <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_Patrick" title="Nicholas Patrick">\n        Nick Patrick\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robert_Behnken" title="Robert Behnken">\n        Bob Behnken\n       </a>\n       get all the tools they need ready for their spacewalk on flight day 5. While Patrick and Behnken were getting the tools ready, commander\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/George_Zamka" title="George Zamka">\n        George Zamka\n       </a>\n       and ISS flight engineer\n       <a href="/wiki/Soichi_Noguchi" title="Soichi Noguchi">\n        Soichi Noguchi\n       </a>\n       swapped out the Hard Upper Torso (HUT) on Bob Behnken\'s suit, since the original HUT had developed a problem with a wire harness and was not powering the Wireless Video System (WVS) or the heaters in his gloves and boots. Once the swap was complete, Zamka and Noguchi tested the suit successfully. The crew also performed a number of transfer related activities during the morning of their work day. After a joint meal together, the crew of STS-130 and ISS commander\n       <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_Williams_(astronaut)" title="Jeffrey Williams (astronaut)">\n        Jeff Williams\n       </a>\n       and flight engineer\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/T.J._Creamer" title="T.J. Creamer">\n        T.J. Creamer\n       </a>\n       conducted a PAO event with T.V. stations in\n       <a href="/wiki/Sacramento,_California" title="Sacramento, California">\n        Sacramento\n       </a>\n       , California,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mobile,_Alabama" title="Mobile, Alabama">\n        Mobile\n       </a>\n       , Alabama and a radio station in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Louis,_Missouri" title="St. Louis, Missouri">\n        St. Louis\n       </a>\n       , Missouri. Once the PAO event was finished, the joint crews had some off duty time for the rest of the day. Before the two crews went to bed they conducted a spacewalk procedures review, then got Nick Patrick and Bob Behnken into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Quest_Joint_Airlock" title="Quest Joint Airlock">\n        Quest Airlock\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Behnken and Patrick spent the night there at 10.2 psi instead of at the station\'s 14.6 psi, breathing pure oxygen for an hour before and after their sleep period in order to prevent\n       <a href="/wiki/Decompression_sickness" title="Decompression sickness">\n        decompression sickness\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="12_February_(Flight_Day_5:_Spacewalk_1)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="12_February_.28Flight_Day_5:_Spacewalk_1.29">\n        12 February (Flight Day 5: Spacewalk 1)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 12 February (Flight Day 5: Spacewalk 1)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2034" data-file-width="3064" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg/220px-STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg/330px-STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ea/STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg/440px-STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_EVA1_Robert_Behnken_and_Nicholas_Patrick_1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Astronauts Behnken and Patrick participate in the first spacewalk.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 5 saw astronauts Nick Patrick and Bob Behnken perform the mission\'s first spacewalk,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which began on time at 02:17 UTC. Their first task was to move the payload bay of\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       and prepare and release launch locks on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Tranquility_(ISS_module)" title="Tranquility (ISS module)">\n        Tranquility module\n       </a>\n       and Cupola. Once Behnken and Patrick were clear of its path, the Tranquility module was moved to the port side of the Unity node using the space station\'s robot arm. Before Tranquility was installed the spacewalkers removed\n       <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n        Dextre\'s\n       </a>\n       ORU platform and secured it to one of the truss segments to function as a backup for a platform to be installed on\n       <a href="/wiki/STS-132" title="STS-132">\n        STS-132\n       </a>\n       . Once the new module was in place, the spacewalkers proceeded to connect temporary heater and data cables between\n       <a href="/wiki/Unity_(ISS_module)" title="Unity (ISS module)">\n        Unity\n       </a>\n       and Tranquility. Behnken and Patrick were ahead of the timeline so they were also able to complete some get-ahead tasks. The spacewalk was completed six and a half hours later, on Friday, 08:49 UTC. After the spacewalk, other crew members completed transfer-related tasks. The transfers are now over halfway complete.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="13_February_(Flight_Day_6:_Spacewalk_2_preparation)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="13_February_.28Flight_Day_6:_Spacewalk_2_preparation.29">\n        13 February (Flight Day 6: Spacewalk 2 preparation)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 13 February (Flight Day 6: Spacewalk 2 preparation)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 6 members of the joint crew opened the hatches to the new Tranquility module for the first time. STS-130 crew-members George Zamka, Terry Virts, Stephen Robinson and Kay Hire all helped in the initial outfitting of the node. During the initial outfitting, Terry Virts and Kay Hire prepared the Cupola for its move from the end of Node 3. While that was going on spacewalkers Bob Behnken and Nick Patrick re-sized and repaired Bob Behnken\'s original suit for use by Nick Patrick, after a small problem with a fan was discovered. Once that task was complete the pair began getting their tools ready for the second of three spacewalks. Throughout the day there were 2 PAO events, the first was a special event conducted by Capcom\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Michael_J._Massimino" title="Michael J. Massimino">\n        Mike Massimino\n       </a>\n       . Massimino asked Bob Behnken and Nick Patrick questions he received through his Twitter account. Later in the day Kay Hire and Terry Virts took questions from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Associated_Press" title="Associated Press">\n        Associated Press\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/CBS_News" title="CBS News">\n        CBS News\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Reuters" title="Reuters">\n        Reuters\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At the end of the day the whole crew conducted another EVA procedures review in preparation for EVA2.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="14_February_(Flight_Day_7:_Spacewalk_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="14_February_.28Flight_Day_7:_Spacewalk_2.29">\n        14 February (Flight Day 7: Spacewalk 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 14 February (Flight Day 7: Spacewalk 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg/220px-STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg/330px-STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg/440px-STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_EVA2_Robert_Behnken_3.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Robert Behnken participates in the second spacewalk.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The second of three spacewalks was completed on flight day 7.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robert_Behnken" title="Robert Behnken">\n        Bob Behnken\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_Patrick" title="Nicholas Patrick">\n        Nick Patrick\n       </a>\n       were able to complete all their planned tasks in 5 hours and 54 minutes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">\n        <a href="#cite_note-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The tasks included installing\n       <a href="/wiki/Ammonia" title="Ammonia">\n        ammonia\n       </a>\n       coolant loops, thermal blankets to protect the ammonia hoses, outfitting the earth facing port of Tranquility for the Cupola, install handrails and a non-propulsive vent valve (NPV). During the connection of one of the ammonia hoses, a small amount of ammonia leaked out of a quick disconnect valve and floated towards Nick Patrick. Procedures called for a "bake-out" while Patrick worked during the sunlit portion of the orbit, and a contamination test in the airlock. The bake-out happened at the end of the spacewalk. While the spacewalk was happening,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Terry_Virts" title="Terry Virts">\n        Terry Virts\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kathryn_Hire" title="Kathryn Hire">\n        Kay Hire\n       </a>\n       along with ISS commander\n       <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_Williams_(astronaut)" title="Jeffrey Williams (astronaut)">\n        Jeff Williams\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Soichi_Noguchi" title="Soichi Noguchi">\n        Soichi Noguchi\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/T.J._Creamer" title="T.J. Creamer">\n        T.J. Creamer\n       </a>\n       , continued outfitting the Tranquility module. This included setting up the ventilation system, connecting electrical and computer cables and configuring racks. They confirmed lights and computers were on in the node once the ammonia cooling system had been activated. The crew also received word the mission had been extended by one day in the morning.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="15_February_(Flight_Day_8)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="15_February_.28Flight_Day_8.29">\n        15 February (Flight Day 8)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 15 February (Flight Day 8)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg/220px-Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg/330px-Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg/440px-Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Canadarm2_Cupola_Relocation_STS_130.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Cupola was moved by Canadarm2 from the forward port to the nadir port of Tranquility.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 8, the Cupola was successfully moved from its launch location to its permanent location on the earth facing side of Tranquility.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Cupola was moved by the space station robot arm (SSRMS), which was operated by Kay Hire and Terry Virts. ISS commander Jeff Williams assisted them by releasing the bolts and hooks that held the Cupola in place and then securing it to its new home. The process was slightly delayed due to some bolts that were torqued tighter than expected on the ground, but flight controllers were able to increase the torque to release the bolts. Once the move of the Cupola was complete, outfitting continued to get the cupola ready. The crew will be able to ingress it tomorrow, but the window covers will not be opened until after the third and final spacewalk. While the Cupola relocation was going on, some of the crew members participated in transferring items between the shuttle and station. Also during this time Bob Behnken and Nick Patrick prepared the tools that they will use during the final spacewalk scheduled for flight day 10. During this time the pair re-sized another spacesuit on station for use by Behnken. This was done because the suit Behnken had been using had some problems with its communications equipment.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="16_February_(Flight_Day_9:_Spacewalk_3_preparation)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="16_February_.28Flight_Day_9:_Spacewalk_3_preparation.29">\n        16 February (Flight Day 9: Spacewalk 3 preparation)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 16 February (Flight Day 9: Spacewalk 3 preparation)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2040" data-file-width="3072" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg/220px-STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg/330px-STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg/440px-STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_PMA-3_relocation_1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Relocation of PMA3 to the end of Tranquility.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Flight day 9 saw the relocation of\n       <a href="/wiki/Pressurized_Mating_Adapter" title="Pressurized Mating Adapter">\n        Pressurized Mating Adapter 3\n       </a>\n       (PMA3) from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Harmony_(ISS_module)" title="Harmony (ISS module)">\n        Harmony node\n       </a>\n       , where it was temporarily located, to its permanent home on the end of Tranquility.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The PMA will provide protection from micro-meteoroids and orbital debris. PMA3 was moved by Bob Behnken and Nick Patrick, with help from Jeff Williams and Soichi Noguchi to release the PMA3. During the PMA3 relocation, Kay Hire and Terry Virts continued work on outfitting the Cupola. The joint Expedition 22/STS-130 crews enjoyed a meal together and had some off-duty time in the 2nd half of their day. Before the scheduled bedtime the entire crew conducted another EVA procedures review for the third and final EVA of the mission.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="17_February_(Flight_Day_10:_Spacewalk_3)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="17_February_.28Flight_Day_10:_Spacewalk_3.29">\n        17 February (Flight Day 10: Spacewalk 3)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 17 February (Flight Day 10: Spacewalk 3)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 10, astronauts Bob Behnken and Nick Patrick completed the third and final spacewalk of the STS-130 mission. Their tasks included hooking up heater and data cables for PMA-3, removing thermal covers and launch locks on Cupola, and installing handrails on Tranquility and a video cable for another base to be installed on the Russian segment of the ISS.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-28">\n        <a href="#cite_note-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Bob Behnken also connected the second ammonia cooling loop and disconnected a temporary power cable on Tranquility. Once the launch locks were removed, pilot Terry Virts opened the windows on Cupola for the first time.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the day Kay Hire and Terry Virts hooked up and transferred the Cupola robotics station for its use in the future. Terry Virts also completed some transfer tasks in the morning.\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center" style="max-width: 652px;_width: 652px;">\n       <li    </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Nick Patrick checking the view from inside.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="18_February_(Flight_Day_11)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="18_February_.28Flight_Day_11.29">\n        18 February (Flight Day 11)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: 18 February (Flight Day 11)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On flight day 11, the joint Expedition 22/STS-130 crew received a phone call from U.S. President\n       <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n        Barack Obama\n       </a>\n       and several school children.After the conference with President Obama and the children, the crew members began transferring\n       <a href="/wiki/ISS_ECLSS" title="ISS ECLSS">\n        Environmental control and life support system\n       </a>\n       (ECLSS) racks to the Tranquility module. These transfers were done by ISS commander Jeff Williams, flight engineer T.J. Creamer, shuttle commander George Zamka and mission specialist Stephen Robinson and took most of the day. Also during the day pilot Terry Virts continued working on getting the Cupola set-up for the robotics work station. He had a small problem installing some corner panels which are needed to hold the workstation. Spacewalkers Bob Behnken and Nick Patrick were busy reconfiguring the airlock for use by the station crew and later flights. They also transferred their spacesuits and tools back to the shuttle for the return trip home. After the rack transfers were done the crew completed some more transfers and passed the 75% complete mark. The space shuttle commanded by commander George Zamka and pilot Terry Virts completed a reboost of the station using its\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vernier_thrusters" title="Vernier thrusters">\n        vernier thrusters\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center" style="max-width: 652px;_width: 652px;">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:15px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:President_Speaks_to_Crew_on_Space_Station.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="3984" data-file-width="2642" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/President_Speaks_to_Crew_on_Space_Station.jpg/79px-President_Speaks_to_Crew_on_Space_Station.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/President_Speaks_to_Crew_on_Space_Station.jpg/119px-President_Speaks_to_Crew_on_Space_Station.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/President_Speaks_to_Crew_on_Space_Station.jpg/159px-President_Speaks_to_Crew_on_Space_Station.jpg 2x" width="79"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           President\n           <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n            Obama\n           </a>\n           during a call to the crew on flight day 11.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_Crew_in_the_Cupola.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/STS-130_Crew_in_the_Cupola.jpg/120px-STS-130_Crew_in_the_Cupola.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/STS-130_Crew_in_the_Cupola.jpg/180px-STS-130_Crew_in_the_Cupola.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/75/STS-130_Crew_in_the_Cupola.jpg/240px-STS-130_Crew_in_the_Cupola.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           STS 130 crew members pose for a portrait in the cupola\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="19_February_(Flight_Day_12)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="19_February_.28Flight_Day_12.29">\n        19 February (Flight Day 12)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 19 February (Flight Day 12)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The STS-130 crew completed their remaining transfer tasks on flight day 12. The joint STS-130/Expedition 22 crew held a joint press conference with reports at NASA centers and in Japan. ISS commander Jeff Williams and shuttle commander George Zamka held a ribbon cutting ceremony to officially open the cupola for use.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After the conference and ribbon cutting ceremony the crews gathered one last time for a meal together in the Unity module. After their meal the crews conducted a farewell ceremony and closed the hatches between the two vehicles.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n        <a href="#cite_note-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The latter part of the STS-130 crew\'s day was spent stowing items and getting their rendezvous tools out and checking them out to ensure they are ready for undocking.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="20_February_(Flight_Day_13_\xe2\x80\x93_Undocking)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="20_February_.28Flight_Day_13_.E2.80.93_Undocking.29">\n        20 February (Flight Day 13 \xe2\x80\x93 Undocking)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 20 February (Flight Day 13 \xe2\x80\x93 Undocking)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       successfully undocked with the ISS at 00:54 UTC (19:54 EST) on flight day 13. After undocking, pilot Terry Virts backed\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       to a distance of 400 feet (120\xc2\xa0m) and began conducting a fly around of the ISS. After the fly around was complete, Virts used\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\'s\n       </i>\n       jets to move the shuttle to a point behind the station. Once the separation burns were complete, the crew conducted the late inspection of the shuttles thermal protection system. The inspection took up most of the crews afternoon with crew members rotating in and out to help with it.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-undock_34-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-undock-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Commander George Zamka performed a waste water and condensate water dump, with the help of Terry Virts.\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c4/ISSpoststs130.jpg/240px-ISSpoststs130.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           The newly upgraded International Space Station seen from the shuttle after undocking.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/STS-130_Endeavour_flyaround10.jpg/240px-STS-130_Endeavour_flyaround10.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Endeavour\n           </i>\n           seen from the International Space Station after undocking\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/03/Port_Side_of_Endeavour%27s_Cargo_Bay_STS_130.jpg/240px-Port_Side_of_Endeavour%27s_Cargo_Bay_STS_130.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Port side of Endeavour\'s cargo bay after undocking.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="21_February_(Flight_Day_14:_Landing_Prep)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="21_February_.28Flight_Day_14:_Landing_Prep.29">\n        21 February (Flight Day 14: Landing Prep)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 21 February (Flight Day 14: Landing Prep)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The crew of STS-130 began preparing the space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       for landing.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the day commander George Zamka and pilot Terry Virts, with help from mission specialist and flight engineer Stephen Robinson checked out the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Flight_Control_System" title="Flight Control System">\n        Flight Control System\n       </a>\n       (FCS) and did a hot fire test of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Reaction_Control_System" title="Reaction Control System">\n        Reaction Control System\n       </a>\n       (RCS). Commander Zamka also did communications checks with mission control through the tracking stations at\n       <a href="/wiki/Merritt_Island_Spaceflight_Tracking_and_Data_Network_station" title="Merritt Island Spaceflight Tracking and Data Network station">\n        Merit Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/White_Sands_Space_Harbor" title="White Sands Space Harbor">\n        White Sands Space Harbor\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Edwards_Air_Force_Base" title="Edwards Air Force Base">\n        Edwards Air Force Base\n       </a>\n       . These checks are routine for the day before landing and were all successful. While all the system checkouts were going on, the rest of the crew were stowing items no longer needed during the flight. During the early part of the day Stephen Robinson and Terry Virts also stowed and deactivated the space shuttle robotic arm. The entire crew also took time out of their day to conduct an in-flight interview with\n       <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">\n        CNN\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CNN_Espa%C3%B1ol" title="CNN Espa\xc3\xb1ol">\n        CNN Espa\xc3\xb1ol\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Univision" title="Univision">\n        Univision\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FD14_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FD14-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="22_February_(Flight_Day_15:_Landing)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="22_February_.28Flight_Day_15:_Landing.29">\n        22 February (Flight Day 15: Landing)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 22 February (Flight Day 15: Landing)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_2" style="width:220px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:480px"&gt;&lt;video id="mwe_player_3" poster="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-130_landing.ogv/480px--STS-130_landing.ogv.jpg" controls="" preload="none" autoplay="" style="width:480px;height:270px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="178.15217687075" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="STS-130_landing.ogv" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/89/STS-130_landing.ogv" type="video/ogg; codecs=&amp;quot;vorbis, theora&amp;quot;" data-title="Original Ogg file, 480 \xc3\x97 270 (493 kbps)" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-width="480" data-height="270" data-bandwidth="493239" data-framerate="29.97002997003"/&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/8/89/STS-130_landing.ogv/STS-130_landing.ogv.160p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="Low bandwidth WebM (160P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 160P" data-transcodekey="160p.webm" data-width="284" data-height="160" data-bandwidth="198056" data-framerate="29.97002997003"/&gt;&lt;source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/8/89/STS-130_landing.ogv/STS-130_landing.ogv.240p.webm" type="video/webm; codecs=&amp;quot;vp8, vorbis&amp;quot;" data-title="Small WebM (240P)" data-shorttitle="WebM 240P" data-transcodekey="240p.webm" data-width="426" data-height="240" data-bandwidth="318920" data-framerate="29.97002997003"/&gt;&lt;/video&gt;&lt;/div&gt;\'>\n         <img alt="File:STS-130 landing.ogv" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/STS-130_landing.ogv/220px-seek%3D65-STS-130_landing.ogv.jpg" style="width:220px;height:124px"/>\n         <a href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/89/STS-130_landing.ogv" target="new" title="Play media">\n          <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:STS-130_landing.ogv" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <b>\n          Landing video\n         </b>\n         (2 mins 57 secs)\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Space shuttle\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       and her STS-130 crew awoke on flight day 15 to begin getting ready for landing. The landing preparations included closing the payload bay doors, activating the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Auxiliary_Power_Unit" title="Auxiliary Power Unit">\n        Auxiliary Power Units\n       </a>\n       and getting into their launch and entry suits. Commander George Zamka and pilot Terry Virts fired\n       <i>\n        Endeavours\n       </i>\n       2\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orbital_Maneuvering_System" title="Orbital Maneuvering System">\n        OMS engines\n       </a>\n       for 2\xc2\xa0mins 38\xc2\xa0secs, this slowed\n       <i>\n        Endeavour\n       </i>\n       by about 200\xc2\xa0ft/s (140\xc2\xa0mph). The decision to go ahead with the de-orbit burn was made 25\xc2\xa0min prior to the burn occurring. Landing occurred at 22:22:10 EST at the\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\'s\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Shuttle_Landing_Facility" title="Shuttle Landing Facility">\n        Shuttle Landing Facility\n       </a>\n       runway 15.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-37">\n        <a href="#cite_note-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38">\n        <a href="#cite_note-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The crew exited the orbiter and inspected it about two hours after landing. All six crew members spoke to the press on the runway before heading back to the Operations &amp; Check-out building.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-landing_39-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-landing-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n the Cupola.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb"      Duration\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Robert_L._Behnken" title="Robert L. Behnken">\n          Robert L. Behnken\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_Patrick" title="Nicholas Patrick">\n          Nicholas Patrick\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         12 February 2010\n         <br/>\n         2:17 UTC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         12 February 2010\n         <br/>\n         8:49 UTC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6 hours 32 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Behnken and Patrick removed a protective cover on a port on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Unity_(ISS_module)" title="Unity (ISS module)">\n          Unity node\n         </a>\n         where Tranquility will be berthed halfway through the spacewalk. They then moved on to release launch locks and connects on Tranquility that connected it to the shuttle. The pair then removed a spare parts platform from\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Special_Purpose_Dexterous_Manipulator" title="Special Purpose Dexterous Manipulator">\n          Special Purpose Dexterous Manipulator\n         </a>\n         or Dextre that will be replaced by a new one on a future mission. Once that task was completed Behnken and Patrick then made several connections on the newly installed Tranquility node to bring it to life.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 2\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Robert L. Behnken\n         <br/>\n         Nicholas Patrick\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         14 February 2010\n         <br/>\n         2:20 UTC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         14 February 2010\n         <br/>\n         8:14 UTC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         5 hours 54 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Behnken and Patrick installed ammonia plumbing and connectors between Unity,\n         <a href="/wiki/Destiny_(ISS_module)" title="Destiny (ISS module)">\n          Destiny\n         </a>\n         and Tranquility and cover them with thermal insulation. When turned on, the ammonia will provide cooling to Tranquility. They then prepared a port on the Earth-facing side of Tranquility for the flight day 8 relocation and attachment of the cupola.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 3\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Nicholas Patrick\n         <br/>\n         Robert L. Behnken\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         17 February 2010\n         <br/>\n         2:15 UTC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         17 February 2010\n         <br/>\n         8:03 UTC\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         5 hours 48 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Behnken and Patrick turned on the ammonia cooling lines between Unity and Tranquility, installed heater and data cables on Tranquility, removed insulation and launch locks from the newly installed Cupola, and installed handrails on the outside of Tranquility.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Wake-up_calls">\n        Wake-up calls\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-130&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Wake-up calls">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       NASA began a tradition of playing music to astronauts during the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gemini_program" title="Gemini program">\n        Gemini program\n       </a>\n       , which was first used to wake up a flight crew during\n       <a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">\n        Apollo 15\n       </a>\n       . Each track is specially chosen, often by their families, and usually has a special meaning to an individual member of the crew, or is applicable to their daily activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chronology_41-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-chronology-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wakeup_42-0">\n
